          $(document).on('change','.order-co-location-plans',function(){
            var element_id = $(this).attr("id");
            var id = $(this).val();

            if(id=="")
            {
                if($(this).parent().parent().find("#error").get(0) === undefined)
                {
                    var err_html = '<span class="error-text help-block help-block-error" id="error"><p class="help-block help-block-error">Plan cannot be blank.</p></span>';
                    $(this).parent().parent().append(err_html);

                    $(this).parent().parent().find("#error p").show();
                }
                else
                {
                    $(this).parent().parent().find("#error p").show();
                }
                return_flag = false;
            }
            else
            {
                $(this).parent().parent().find("#error p").hide();
            }

            var requestData = {id:id,product:'co-location'};
            var selected_row = $(this).data('row');
            ajaxCall('/selfcare/order/get-order-iaas-plans-details', 'POST', requestData, function(data){

                var deviceSpec = data.deviceSpec;
                var title = data.title;
                var deviceSpec = data.deviceSpec;
                var nrc = data.nrc;
                var monthly_rental = data.monthly_rental;
                var default_power = data.default_power;
                var max_power = data.max_power;
                var addl_power_array = data.addl_power_array;
                var first_power = data.first_power;

                var addl_power_array = data.addl_power_array;

                var addl_power_co_location_id = element_id.replace("order-co-location-plans","addl_power_co_location");

                var parent = $("#"+addl_power_co_location_id).parent().parent();
                $("#"+addl_power_co_location_id).parent().remove();
                var html = '<select id="'+addl_power_co_location_id+'" class="custom-select cust-select form-select addl_power_co_location" name="LeadProduct[power_value][]" aria-required="true">'+addl_power_array+'</option>';
                $(parent).append(html);

                loadManualCustomSelectOptions(addl_power_co_location_id);

                $("#"+addl_power_co_location_id).prop("checked", false);

                var remote_hands_on_co_location_display_id = element_id.replace("order-co-location-plans","remote_hands_on_co_location_display");
                $("#"+remote_hands_on_co_location_display_id).html('No');


                var addl_power_co_location_display_id = element_id.replace("order-co-location-plans","addl_power_co_location_display");
                $("#"+addl_power_co_location_display_id).html(first_power);

                id = element_id.replace("order-co-location-plans","monthly_rental");
                $("#"+id).val(data.monthly_rental);

                id = element_id.replace("order-co-location-plans","nrc");
                $("#"+id).val(data.nrc);

                if($("#" + "summary-card-features"+selected_row).length == 0) {
                  var html ='<div id="summary-card-features'+selected_row+'">';
                  html = html + '<ul class="summary-card-features summary-card-package-header">';
                  html = html + '<li><span class="summary-head"><a href="#">';
                  if(selected_row==1)
                    html = html + '<i class="icon-delete-filled"></i>';
                  else
                    html = html + '<i onClick="deleteIaasPlan('+selected_row+')" class="icon-delete-filled"></i>';
                  html = html + '</a><h2 id="package_name'+selected_row+'">'+title+'</h2></span><span class="qty-desk-icon"><h3>Qty.: <span id="quantity'+selected_row+'">1</span></h3></span></li>';
                  html = html + '</ul>';
                  html = html + '<div class="summary-card-package-amount"><span id="plan_amount'+selected_row+'">'+monthly_rental+'</span> BHD/Month</div>';
                  html = html + '<div class="summary-card-package-detail" id="package_details'+selected_row+'">'+deviceSpec+'</div></div>';

                  $("#iaas_aummary").append(html);
                }
                else
                {
                  var iaas_quantity = $("#iaas_quantity"+selected_row).val();
                  $("#package_name"+selected_row).html(title);
                  $("#quantity"+selected_row).html(iaas_quantity);
                  $("#plan_amount"+selected_row).html(monthly_rental);
                  $("#package_details"+selected_row).html(deviceSpec);
                  $("#iaas_quantity"+selected_row).html(iaas_quantity);
                }

                calculateIaasTotal();
            });
          });

          $(document).on('change','.addl_power_co_location',function(){
            var element_id = $(this).attr("id");

          });

          $(document).on('change','.remote_hands_on_co_location',function(){
            var element_id = $(this).attr("id");
            var remote_hands_on_co_location_display_id = element_id.replace("remote_hands_on_co_location","remote_hands_on_co_location_display");
            var id = element_id.replace("remote_hands_on_co_location","remote_hands_on_co_location_value");
            if($(this).prop("checked")==true)
            {
                $("#"+remote_hands_on_co_location_display_id).html("Yes");
                $("#"+id).val("Yes");
            }
            else
            {
                $("#"+remote_hands_on_co_location_display_id).html("No");
                $("#"+id).val("No");
            }
          });

          $(document).on('change','.iaas-operating-system',function(){
            var element_id = $(this).attr("id");
            var id = $(this).val();
            var product = $(this).data("product");
            var requestData = {id:id,product:product};
            var selected_row = $(this).data('row');
            ajaxCall('/selfcare/order/get-iaas-operating-system-details', 'POST', requestData, function(data){
                var price = data.price;
                var price_per_vcpu = data.price_per_vcpu;
                var pricing_for_units = data.pricing_for_units;

                var os_price_id = element_id.replace("iaas-operating-system","os_price");
                var os_price_per_vcpu_id = element_id.replace("iaas-operating-system","os_price_per_vcpu");
                var os_pricing_for_units_id = element_id.replace("iaas-operating-system","os_pricing_for_units");

                $("#"+os_price_id).val(price);
                $("#"+os_price_per_vcpu_id).val(price_per_vcpu);
                $("#"+os_pricing_for_units_id).val(pricing_for_units);

                calculateIaasTotal();
            });
          });

          $(document).on('change','.order-iaas-plans',function(){
            var id = $(this).val();
            if(id=="")
            {
                $("#order-select-plan").parent().parent().find("#error p").html("").hide();
                if($(this).parent().parent().find("#error").get(0) === undefined)
                {
                    var err_html = '<span class="error-text help-block help-block-error" id="error"><p class="help-block help-block-error">Plan cannot be blank.</p></span>';
                    $(this).parent().parent().append(err_html);

                    $(this).parent().parent().find("#error p").show();
                }
                else
                {
                    $(this).parent().parent().find("#error p").show();
                }
            }
            else
            {
                $(this).parent().parent().find("#error p").hide();
            }
            var product = $(this).data("product");
            var requestData = {id:id,product:product};
            var selected_id = $(this).attr('id');
            var selected_row = $(this).data('row');
            ajaxCall('/selfcare/order/get-order-iaas-plans-details', 'POST', requestData, function(data){
              var deviceSpec = data.deviceSpec;
              var title = data.title;
              var deviceSpec = data.deviceSpec;
              var nrc = data.nrc;
              var monthly_rental = data.monthly_rental;

              var default_vcpu = data.default_vcpu;
              var max_vcpu = data.max_vcpu;
              var default_ram = data.default_ram;
              var max_ram = data.max_ram;
              var default_storage = data.default_storage;
              var max_storage = data.max_storage;
              var default_internet = data.default_internet;
              var max_internet = data.max_internet;
              var default_firewall = data.default_firewall;

              var id = selected_id.replace("order-iaas-plans","default_vcpu");
              $("#"+id).val(default_vcpu);

              id = selected_id.replace("order-iaas-plans","max_vcpu");
              $("#"+id).val(data.max_vcpu);

              id = selected_id.replace("order-iaas-plans","default_ram");
              $("#"+id).val(data.default_ram);

              id = selected_id.replace("order-iaas-plans","max_ram");
              $("#"+id).val(data.max_ram);

              id = selected_id.replace("order-iaas-plans","default_storage");
              $("#"+id).val(data.default_storage);

              id = selected_id.replace("order-iaas-plans","max_storage");
              $("#"+id).val(data.max_storage);

              id = selected_id.replace("order-iaas-plans","default_internet");
              default_internet = (default_internet=="")?0:default_internet;
              $("#"+id).val(default_internet);

              id = selected_id.replace("order-iaas-plans","max_internet");
              $("#"+id).val(data.max_internet);

              id = selected_id.replace("order-iaas-plans","default_firewall");
              $("#"+id).val(data.default_firewall);

              id = selected_id.replace("order-iaas-plans","monthly_rental");
              $("#"+id).val(data.monthly_rental);

              id = selected_id.replace("order-iaas-plans","nrc");
              $("#"+id).val(data.nrc);

              var max_vcpu = data.max_vcpu;
              var max_ram = data.max_ram;
              var max_internet = data.max_internet;
              var default_storage = data.default_storage;
              var default_firewall = data.default_firewall;

              id = selected_id.replace("order-iaas-plans","firewall");
              $("#"+id).val(default_storage);
              var firewall_display = "No";

              if(parseInt(default_firewall)!=0)
              {
                id = selected_id.replace("order-iaas-plans","firewall");
                $("#"+id).prop("checked",true);
                firewall_display = "Yes";
              }
              else
              {
                $("#"+id).prop("checked",false);
                firewall_display = "No";
              }

              var option = '';
              for(var i=0;i<max_vcpu;)
              {
                option = option + '<option value="'+i+'">'+i+'</option>';
                i = parseInt(i) + 2;
              }
              id = selected_id.replace("order-iaas-plans","vCPU_select");
              $("#"+id).html(option);

              if($("#"+id).hasClass("cust-select"))
              {
                loadCustomSelectOptions(id);
              }
              else
              {
                $("#"+id).addClass("cust-select");
                loadManualCustomSelectOptions(id);
              }

              option = '';
              for(var i=0;i<=max_ram;i++)
              {
                option = option + '<option value="'+i+'">'+i+'</option>';
              }
              id = selected_id.replace("order-iaas-plans","ram_select");
              $("#"+id).html(option);

              if($("#"+id).hasClass("cust-select"))
              {
                loadCustomSelectOptions(id);
              }
              else
              {
                $("#"+id).addClass("cust-select");
                loadManualCustomSelectOptions(id);
              }


              option = '';
              for(var i=0;i<=max_internet;i++)
              {
                option = option + '<option value="'+i+'">'+i+'</option>';
              }
              id = selected_id.replace("order-iaas-plans","internet_select");
              $("#"+id).html(option);

              if($("#"+id).hasClass("cust-select"))
              {
                loadCustomSelectOptions(id);
              }
              else
              {
                $("#"+id).addClass("cust-select");
                loadManualCustomSelectOptions(id);
              }

              id = selected_id.replace("order-iaas-plans","vCPU_select_display");
              $("#"+id).html(default_vcpu);

              id = selected_id.replace("order-iaas-plans","ram_select_display");
              $("#"+id).html(default_ram);

              id = selected_id.replace("order-iaas-plans","storage_display");
              $("#"+id).html(default_storage);

              id = selected_id.replace("order-iaas-plans","internet_select_display");
              default_internet = (default_internet=="")?0:default_internet;
              $("#"+id).html(default_internet);

              id = selected_id.replace("order-iaas-plans","firewall_display");
              $("#"+id).html(firewall_display);


              loadCustomSelectOptions('ram_select');
              loadCustomSelectOptions('internet_select');

              if($("#" + "summary-card-features"+selected_row).length == 0) {
                if(title!==undefined)
                {
                    var html ='<div id="summary-card-features'+selected_row+'">';
                    html = html + '<ul class="summary-card-features summary-card-package-header">';
                    html = html + '<li><span class="summary-head"><a href="#">';
                    html = html + '<i onClick="deleteIaasPlan('+selected_row+')" class="icon-delete-filled"></i>';
                    html = html + '</a><h2 id="package_name'+selected_row+'">'+title+'</h2></span><span class="qty-desk-icon"><h3>Qty.: <span id="quantity'+selected_row+'">1</span></h3></span></li>';
                    html = html + '</ul>';
                    html = html + '<div class="summary-card-package-amount"><span id="plan_amount'+selected_row+'">'+monthly_rental+'</span> BHD/Month</div>';
                    html = html + '<div class="summary-card-package-detail" id="package_details'+selected_row+'">'+deviceSpec+'</div></div>';

                    $("#iaas_aummary").append(html);
                }
              }
              else
              {
                var iaas_quantity = $("#iaas_quantity"+selected_row).val();
                $("#package_name"+selected_row).html(title);
                $("#quantity"+selected_row).html(iaas_quantity);
                $("#plan_amount"+selected_row).html(monthly_rental);
                $("#package_details"+selected_row).html(deviceSpec);
                $("#iaas_quantity"+selected_row).html(iaas_quantity);
              }

              calculateIaasTotal();
            });
          });


          $(document).on('change','.iaas_quantity',function(){
            var quantity = $(this).val();
            var element_id = $(this).attr("id");
            var quantity_id =  element_id.replace("iaas_quantity","quantity");
            $("#"+quantity_id).html(quantity);
            var sum_quantity = 0;
            $('.iaas_quantity').each(function(){
                sum_quantity += parseInt($(this).val());  // Or this.innerHTML, this.innerText
            });
            $("#quantity_mob").html(sum_quantity)
            calculateIaasTotal();
          });


          $(document).on('change','.vCPU_select',function(){
            var id = $(this).attr("id").replace("vCPU_select","vCPU_select_display");

            var def_id = $(this).attr("id").replace("vCPU_select","default_vcpu");

            var final = parseInt($(this).val()) + parseInt($("#"+def_id).val());

            $("#"+id).html(final);

            calculateIaasTotal();
          });

          $(document).on('change','.ram_select',function(){
            //$("#ram_select_display").html($(this).val());
            var id = $(this).attr("id").replace("ram_select","ram_select_display");

            var def_id = $(this).attr("id").replace("ram_select","default_ram");

            var final = parseInt($(this).val()) + parseInt($("#"+def_id).val());
            $("#"+id).html(final);
          });

          $(document).on('change','.firewall',function(){
            var disp = "No";
            if($(this).prop("checked"))
            {
              disp = "Yes";
            }
            //$("#firewall_display").html($(this).val());
            var id = $(this).attr("id").replace("firewall","firewall_display");
            $("#"+id).html(disp);
            id = $(this).attr("id").replace("firewall","firewall_checked");
            $("#"+id).val(disp);
          });

          $(document).on('change','.iaas_storage',function(){
            var id = $(this).attr("id").replace("iaas_storage","max_storage");
            var max_storage = $("#"+id).val();
            var entered = $(this).val();

            id = $(this).attr("id").replace("iaas_storage","default_storage");
            var default_storage = $("#"+id).val();
            var display_value = default_storage;
            if(parseFloat(entered) > parseFloat(max_storage))
            {
              alert("Storage can not be greater than "+max_storage+" GB");
              display_value = 0;
            }
            else
            {
              //$("#storage_display").html(entered);
              display_value = entered;
            }

            var def_id = $(this).attr("id").replace("iaas_storage","default_storage");

            var final_display_value = parseInt(display_value) + parseInt($("#"+def_id).val());

            id = $(this).attr("id").replace("iaas_storage","storage_display");
            $("#"+id).html(final_display_value);

            $(this).val(display_value);
          });

          $(document).on('change','.internet_select',function(){
            //$("#internet_select_display").html($(this).val());
            var id = $(this).attr("id").replace("internet_select","internet_select_display");
            var def_id = $(this).attr("id").replace("internet_select","default_internet");
            var default_value = $("#"+def_id).val();
            var final = parseInt($(this).val());
            if(!isNaN(default_value) && default_value!="")
            {
                final = parseInt($(this).val()) + parseInt(default_value);
            }
            $("#"+id).html(final);
          });

          $("#order-device-storage").change(function(data){
            var deviceid = $("#order-plan-devices").val();
            var id = $(this).val();
            var device_type = $('#order-plan-devices-types').val();
            var product = $(this).data('product');
            var requestData = {id: id,product:product,device_type:device_type,deviceid:deviceid};
            ajaxCall('/selfcare/order/get-device-payment-plans', 'POST', requestData, function(data){
              if(device_type!="Wifi extender" && device_type!="Wifi+extender") {
                $('#order-device-plans').html(data.responseText);
                loadCustomSelectOptions('order-device-plans');

                $("#order-device-plans").trigger('change');
              }
            });

            orderCalculateTotal();

          });

          $('#order-plan-devices-protect').change(function(){
          var id = $(this).val();
          var requestData = {id: id};
          var deviceProtect =$( "#order-plan-devices-protect option:selected" ).text();
          $('#order-select-plan').append('<input  type="hidden" name="device_protect_name" value="'+deviceProtect+'" />');
          ajaxCall('/selfcare/order/deviceprotect-details', 'POST', requestData, function(data) {
            //alert(data.responseText);
            $('#sidebar-device-protect-details').html(data.responseText);
            orderCalculateTotal();
          });

        });

    function onSubmitValidate(product)
    {
        if(product=="advanced_internet")
        {
            var order_plan_cocntracts = $("#order-plan-cocntracts").val();
            var order_select_plan = $("#order-select-plan").val();

            if(order_plan_cocntracts=="")
            {
                $("#order-plan-cocntracts").parent().parent().find("#error p").html("Please select contract.").show();
            }
            else
            {
                $("#order-plan-cocntracts").parent().parent().find("#error p").html("").hide();
            }

            if(order_select_plan=="")
            {
               $("#order-select-plan").parent().parent().find("#error p").html("Plan cannot be blank.").show();
            }
            else
            {
                $("#order-select-plan").parent().parent().find("#error p").html("").hide();
            }
            if(order_plan_cocntracts=="" || order_select_plan=="")
            {
                return false;
            }
        }
        else if(product=='iaas' || product=='draas')
        {
            var order_iaas_plans = document.getElementsByClassName('order-iaas-plans');
            var iaas_operating_systems = document.getElementsByClassName('iaas-operating-system');
            var return_flag = true;
            for(var i=0;i<order_iaas_plans.length;i++) {
                var order_iaas_plan = order_iaas_plans[i].value;
                var iaas_operating_system = iaas_operating_systems[i].value;

                if(order_iaas_plan=="")
                {
                    return_flag = false;
                    if($(order_iaas_plans[i]).parent().parent().find("#error").get(0) === undefined)
                    {
                        var err_html = '<span class="error-text help-block help-block-error" id="error"><p class="help-block help-block-error">Please select plan.</p></span>';
                        $(order_iaas_plans[i]).parent().parent().append(err_html);

                        $(order_iaas_plans[i]).parent().parent().find("#error p").show();
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        $(order_iaas_plans[i]).parent().parent().find("#error p").show();
                    }
                }
                else
                {
                    $(order_iaas_plans[i]).parent().parent().find("#error p").hide();
                }

                if(iaas_operating_system=="")
                {
                    if($(iaas_operating_systems[i]).parent().parent().find("#error").get(0) === undefined)
                    {
                        var err_html = '<span class="error-text help-block help-block-error" id="error"><p class="help-block help-block-error">Please select operating system.</p></span>';
                        $(iaas_operating_systems[i]).parent().parent().append(err_html);

                        $(iaas_operating_systems[i]).parent().parent().find("#error p").show();
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        $(iaas_operating_systems[i]).parent().parent().find("#error p").show();
                    }
                    return_flag = false;
                }
                else
                {
                    $(iaas_operating_systems[i]).parent().parent().find("#error p").hide();
                }
            }

            return return_flag;
        }
        else if(product=='baas')
        {
            var order_iaas_plans = document.getElementsByClassName('order-iaas-plans');
            var return_flag = true;
            for(var i=0;i<order_iaas_plans.length;i++) {
                var order_iaas_plan = order_iaas_plans[i].value;

                if(order_iaas_plan=="")
                {
                    return_flag = false;
                    if($(order_iaas_plans[i]).parent().parent().find("#error").get(0) === undefined)
                    {
                        var err_html = '<span class="error-text help-block help-block-error" id="error"><p class="help-block help-block-error">Please select plan.</p></span>';
                        $(order_iaas_plans[i]).parent().parent().append(err_html);

                        $(order_iaas_plans[i]).parent().parent().find("#error p").show();
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        $(order_iaas_plans[i]).parent().parent().find("#error p").show();
                    }
                }
                else
                {
                    $(order_iaas_plans[i]).parent().parent().find("#error p").hide();
                }
            }

            return return_flag;
        }
        else if(product=='unified_comm' || product=='videoconf')
        {
            var order_plan_cocntracts = $("#order-plan-cocntracts").val();
            var order_select_plan = $("#order-select-plan").val();
            var return_flag = true;
            if(order_plan_cocntracts=="")
            {
                if($("#order-plan-cocntracts").parent().parent().find("#error").get(0) === undefined)
                {
                    var err_html = '<span class="error-text help-block help-block-error" id="error"><p class="help-block help-block-error">Please select contract.</p></span>';
                    $("#order-plan-cocntracts").parent().parent().append(err_html);

                    $("#order-plan-cocntracts").parent().parent().find("#error p").show();
                }
                else
                {
                    $("#order-plan-cocntracts").parent().parent().find("#error p").show();
                }
                return_flag = false;
            }
            else
            {
                $("#order-plan-cocntracts").parent().parent().find("#error p").hide();
            }

            if(order_select_plan=="")
            {
                if($("#order-select-plan").parent().parent().find("#error").get(0) === undefined)
                {
                    var err_html = '<span class="error-text help-block help-block-error" id="error"><p class="help-block help-block-error">Please select plan.</p></span>';
                    $("#order-select-plan").parent().parent().append(err_html);

                    $("#order-select-plan").parent().parent().find("#error p").show();
                }
                else
                {
                    $("#order-select-plan").parent().parent().find("#error p").show();
                }
                return_flag = false;
            }
            else
            {
                $("#order-select-plan").parent().parent().find("#error p").hide();
            }

            return return_flag;
        }
        else if(product=='co-location')
        {
            var order_iaas_plans = document.getElementsByClassName('order-co-location-plans');

            var return_flag = true;
            for(var i=0;i<order_iaas_plans.length;i++) {
                var order_iaas_plan = order_iaas_plans[i].value;
                if(order_iaas_plan=="")
                {
                    if($(order_iaas_plans[i]).parent().parent().find("#error").get(0) === undefined)
                    {
                        var err_html = '<span class="error-text help-block help-block-error" id="error"><p class="help-block help-block-error">Please select plan.</p></span>';
                        $(order_iaas_plans[i]).parent().parent().append(err_html);

                        $(order_iaas_plans[i]).parent().parent().find("#error p").show();
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        $(order_iaas_plans[i]).parent().parent().find("#error p").show();
                    }
                    return_flag = false;
                }
                else
                {
                    $(order_iaas_plans[i]).parent().parent().find("#error p").hide();
                }
            }
            return return_flag;
        }
        else if(product=='bb')
        {
            var order_plan_cocntracts = $("#order-plan-cocntracts").val();
            var order_select_plan = $("#order-select-plan").val();

            var order_plan_devices = $("#order-plan-devices").val();

            var return_flag = true;
            if(order_plan_cocntracts=="")
            {
                if($("#order-plan-cocntracts").parent().parent().find("#error").get(0) === undefined)
                {
                    var err_html = '<span class="error-text help-block help-block-error" id="error"><p class="help-block help-block-error">Please select contract.</p></span>';
                    $("#order-plan-cocntracts").parent().parent().append(err_html);

                    $("#order-plan-cocntracts").parent().parent().find("#error p").show();
                }
                else
                {
                    $("#order-plan-cocntracts").parent().parent().find("#error p").show();
                }
                return_flag = false;
            }
            else
            {
                $("#order-plan-cocntracts").parent().parent().find("#error p").hide();
            }

            if(order_select_plan=="")
            {
                if($("#order-select-plan").parent().parent().find("#error").get(0) === undefined)
                {
                    var err_html = '<span class="error-text help-block help-block-error" id="error"><p class="help-block help-block-error">Please select plan.</p></span>';
                    $("#order-select-plan").parent().parent().append(err_html);

                    $("#order-select-plan").parent().parent().find("#error p").show();
                }
                else
                {
                    $("#order-select-plan").parent().parent().find("#error p").show();
                }
                return_flag = false;
            }
            else
            {
                $("#order-select-plan").parent().parent().find("#error p").hide();
            }

           /* if(order_plan_devices=="")
            {
                if($("#order-plan-devices").parent().parent().find("#error").get(0) === undefined)
                {
                    var err_html = '<span class="error-text help-block help-block-error" id="error"><p class="help-block help-block-error">Please select device.</p></span>';
                    $("#order-plan-devices").parent().parent().append(err_html);

                    $("#order-plan-devices").parent().parent().find("#error p").show();
                }
                else
                {
                    $("#order-plan-devices").parent().parent().find("#error p").show();
                }
                return_flag = false;
            }
            else
            {
                $("#order-plan-devices").parent().parent().find("#error p").hide();
            }*/

            return return_flag;
        }
        else if(product=='dia' || product=='localmpls')
        {
            var order_plan_cocntracts = $("#order-plan-cocntracts").val();
            var order_plan_downloadSpeed = $("#order-plan-downloadSpeed").val();
            var leadproduct_quantity = $("#leadproduct-quantity").val();

            var return_flag = true;
            if(order_plan_cocntracts=="")
            {
                if($("#order-plan-cocntracts").parent().parent().find("#error").get(0) === undefined)
                {
                    var err_html = '<span class="error-text help-block help-block-error" id="error"><p class="help-block help-block-error">Please select contract.</p></span>';
                    $("#order-plan-cocntracts").parent().parent().append(err_html);

                    $("#order-plan-cocntracts").parent().parent().find("#error p").show();
                }
                else
                {
                    $("#order-plan-cocntracts").parent().parent().find("#error p").show();
                }
                return_flag = false;
            }
            else
            {
                $("#order-plan-cocntracts").parent().parent().find("#error p").hide();
            }

            if(order_plan_downloadSpeed=="")
            {
                if($("#order-plan-downloadSpeed").parent().parent().find("#error").get(0) === undefined)
                {
                    var err_html = '<span class="error-text help-block help-block-error" id="error"><p class="help-block help-block-error">Please select speed.</p></span>';
                    $("#order-plan-downloadSpeed").parent().parent().append(err_html);

                    $("#order-plan-downloadSpeed").parent().parent().find("#error p").show();
                }
                else
                {
                    $("#order-plan-downloadSpeed").parent().parent().find("#error p").show();
                }
                return_flag = false;
            }
            else
            {
                $("#order-plan-downloadSpeed").parent().parent().find("#error p").hide();
            }

            if(leadproduct_quantity=="")
            {
                $("#leadproduct-quantity").parent().parent().find("#error").html("Quantity cannot be blank.");
                return_flag = false;
            }
            else
            {
                $("#leadproduct-quantity").parent().parent().find("#error").html("Quantity cannot be blank.").hide();
            }

            return return_flag;
        }
        return true;
    }


    function orderCalculateTotal() {
        var quantity = 1;
    if($('span#summary-quantity').text()){
        quantity = $('span#summary-quantity').text(); }
    if($('input#order-summary-quantity').val()){
        quantity = $('input#order-summary-quantity').val();
        $('span#summary-quantity').text(quantity);
    }else{
        $('span#summary-quantity').text(0);
    }
    //alert(quantity);
    var quantity1 = $('#order-summary-quantity-1').val();
    var quantity2 = $('#order-summary-quantity-2').val();
    var quantity3 = $('#order-summary-quantity-3').val();
    var quantity4 = $('#order-summary-quantity-4').val();
    var quantity5 = $('#order-summary-quantity-5').val();


    var planAmount = 0; var addonAmount = 0; var deviceAmount = 0; var protectAmount = 0; var nrcAmount=0;
    var plan1Amount = 0; var plan2Amount = 0; var plan3Amount = 0; var plan4Amount = 0; var plan5Amount = 0;
    var quantity1 = 0; var quantity2 = 0; var quantity3 = 0; var quantity4 = 0; var quantity5 = 0; nrcAmount =0;


    if($('span#order-plan-unit-price').text()){ planAmount = $('span#order-plan-unit-price').text(); }
    //alert(planAmount);
    if($('span#order-addon-unit-price').text()){ addonAmount = $('span#order-addon-unit-price').text(); }
    if($('span#order-device-unit-price').text()){ deviceAmount = $('span#order-device-unit-price').text(); }
    if($('span#order-protect-price').text()){ protectAmount = $('span#order-protect-price').text(); }
    if($('#originalNrc').val()){ nrcAmount = $('#originalNrc').val(); }

    if($('span#order-plan-unit-price-1').text()){ plan1Amount = $('span#order-plan-unit-price-1').text(); }
    if($('span#order-plan-unit-price-2').text()){ plan2Amount = $('span#order-plan-unit-price-2').text(); }
    if($('span#order-plan-unit-price-3').text()){ plan3Amount = $('span#order-plan-unit-price-3').text(); }
    if($('span#order-plan-unit-price-4').text()){ plan4Amount = $('span#order-plan-unit-price-4').text(); }
    if($('span#order-plan-unit-price-5').text()){ plan5Amount = $('span#order-plan-unit-price-5').text(); }

    if($('#order-summary-quantity-1').val()){ quantity1 = $('#order-summary-quantity-1').val(); }
    if($('#order-summary-quantity-2').val()){ quantity2 = $('#order-summary-quantity-2').val(); }
    if($('#order-summary-quantity-3').val()){ quantity3 = $('#order-summary-quantity-3').val(); }
    if($('#order-summary-quantity-4').val()){ quantity4 = $('#order-summary-quantity-4').val(); }
    if($('#order-summary-quantity-5').val()){ quantity5 = $('#order-summary-quantity-5').val(); }


    //alert(quantity + ':' + planAmount + ' ** ' + quantity1 + ': ' + plan1Amount + ' ** ' + quantity2 + ': ' + plan2Amount);

    var totalAmount = quantity * ( parseFloat(planAmount) + parseFloat(addonAmount) + parseFloat(deviceAmount) + parseFloat(protectAmount) ) + quantity1 * parseFloat(plan1Amount) + quantity2 * parseFloat(plan2Amount) + quantity3 * parseFloat(plan3Amount) + quantity4 * parseFloat(plan4Amount) + quantity5 * parseFloat(plan5Amount);

//alert(parseFloat(totalAmount) + ' ** ' +parseFloat(planAmount) + ' ** ' + parseFloat(addonAmount) + ' ** '  + parseFloat(deviceAmount) + ' ** '  + parseFloat(protectAmount)+ ' ** '  + parseFloat(quantity)  );
//alert(totalAmount);

/*
    totalAmount = parseFloat(totalAmount) + parseFloat(quantity1) * parseFloat(plan1Amount) + parseFloat(quantity2) * parseFloat(plan2Amount) + parseFloat(quantity3) * parseFloat(plan3Amount) + parseFloat(quantity4) * parseFloat(plan4Amount) + parseFloat(quantity5) * parseFloat(plan5Amount);
alert(totalAmount);
*/

    nrcAmount = quantity * nrcAmount;
    //if($('#order-nrc').val()){ nrcAmount = $('#order-nrc').val(); }
    //var nrcAmount = quantity * parseFloat($('#order-nrc').text());


    $('span#nrc-total').html(parseFloat(nrcAmount).toFixed(2));
    var grantTotal = parseFloat(nrcAmount) + parseFloat(totalAmount);
    //alert(nrcAmount);
    $('#order-nrc').html(parseFloat(nrcAmount).toFixed(2));
    $('#order-monthly-total').html(parseFloat(totalAmount).toFixed(2));
    var order_grand_total =  parseFloat(grantTotal).toFixed(2);
    $('#order-grant-total').html(addCommas(order_grand_total));

//alert(totalAmount);

    $('input.added-input').remove();
    $('#order-select-plan').append('<input class="added-input" type="hidden" name="nrcAmount" value="'+nrcAmount+'" />');
    $('#order-select-plan').append('<input class="added-input" type="hidden" name="totalAmount" value="'+parseFloat(totalAmount)+'" />');
    $('#order-select-plan').append('<input class="added-input" type="hidden" name="grantTotal" value="'+grantTotal+'" />');
  }



</script>

    $(document).on('click','#end_user_checkbox_all',function(){
         if($(this).is(":checked")){
            $("td label.control--checkbox input").not( "li a label.control--checkbox input" ).prop("checked",true);
        }
        else if($(this).is(":not(:checked)")){
            $("td  label.control--checkbox input").not( "li a label.control--checkbox input" ).prop("checked",false);
        }
    });

  });

// add method to display number in unit format
  function addCommas(nStr){
 nStr += '';
 var x = nStr.split('.');
 var x1 = x[0];
 var x2 = x.length > 1 ? '.' + x[1] : '';
 var rgx = /(\d+)(\d{3})/;
 while (rgx.test(x1)) {
  x1 = x1.replace(rgx, '$1' + ',' + '$2');
 }
 return x1 + x2;
}

function check_required_inputs() {
var hasrequirederror = false;
    $('.require').each(function(){
      if( $(this).val() == "" ) {
        $(this).css('border-bottom',"1px solid #ff0000 !important");
        hasrequirederror = true;
        return false;
      }
    });

    if(hasrequirederror) {
      // $('#msg-enter-amount').html('AMOUNT CANNOT BE BLANK');
      return false;
    }
    return true;
}

function forceNumeric(number) {
    return number.each(function () {
     $(this).keydown(function (e) {
         if ($.inArray(e.keyCode, [46, 8, 9, 27, 13, 110, 190]) !== -1 ||
         // Allow: Ctrl+A
        (e.keyCode == 65 && e.ctrlKey === true) ||
         // Allow: Ctrl+C
        (e.keyCode == 67 && e.ctrlKey === true) ||
         // Allow: Ctrl+X
        (e.keyCode == 86 && e.ctrlKey === true) ||
         // Allow: Ctrl+V
        (e.keyCode == 88 && e.ctrlKey === true) ||
        // Allow mobile chrome
        (e.keyCode == 229) ||
         // Allow: home, end, left, right
        (e.keyCode >= 35 && e.keyCode <= 39)) {
             // let it happen, don't do anything
             return;
      }
      //Ensure that it is a number and stop the keypress
      if ((e.shiftKey || (e.keyCode < 48 || e.keyCode > 57)) && (e.keyCode < 96 || e.keyCode > 105)) {
          e.preventDefault();
      }
     });
 });
}

function isNavigationKey(key) {
    return  key == 9 || key == 13 || key == 35 || key == 36 || key == 37 || key == 39; // Tab and Enter, Home and End, left and right arrows
}

  <script>

$( window ).resize(function() {

    var listItems = $(".common-nav .nav-tabs li");
    var liWidth = 0;
    var width = 0;
    var currentVal = $(".common-nav .nav-tabs a.active").html();

    if ($('.common-nav').hasClass('our-solution-main') && document.documentElement.lang.toLowerCase() == 'ar') {
        var index = 0;
        listItems.each(function(idx, li) {
            var productWidth = $(li).width();
            var liValue = $(li).children().html();
            var liMargin = $(li).css('margin-right').split('px')[0];

            // if (document.doc
